A tall fallen temple in a dark woodlands marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen temple lies a large, deteriorated room. It's covered in rubble, dead insects and dirt. Your torch allows you to see broken arrows, rusty swords and skeletal remains, worn and spoiled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed collapsed rooms and pillaged treasuries and soon you enter a humid area. The room is filled with lifelike statues of terrified people. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass a few more passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick wooden door blocks your path. Ash and soot is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.
A tall dark cave in a dark mountain range marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the dark cave lies a small, dusty room. It's covered in remains, crawling insects and dead insects. Your torch allows you to see drawings and symbols on the walls, deteriorated and consumed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the middle. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a ragged area. It's filled with hanging cages which still hold skeletal remains. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass a few more passages, they all look so similar, this whole place is a maze. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A grand metal door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A wide graveyard in a dire thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the graveyard lies a narrow, filthy room. It's covered in cobwebs, dead insects and moss. Your torch allows you to see remnants of sacks, crates and caskets, tattered and ravished by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a humid area. Several stacks of gunpowder barrels are stacked against a wall. A skeleton holding a torch lies before it. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass a few more passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive metal door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.
A short waterfall in a overcast wasteland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the waterfall lies a small, putrid room. It's covered in small bones, roots and rat droppings. Your torch allows you to see a broken tomb, weathered and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a dusty area. There's a seemingly endless hole in the center. Around it are what seem like runes. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass various passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A large wooden door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A minor murky cave in a shady grove marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the murky cave lies a narrow, dusty room. It's covered in large bones, remains and large bones. Your torch allows you to see a pillaged treasury, long lost and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a filthy area. Piles and piles of gold lie in the center, several skeletons lie next to it. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass a few more passages, some of them have collapsed, others seem to go on forever. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An enormous metal door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.
A wide pair of granite doors in a gloomy cliff side marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the pair of granite doors lies a large, crumbling room. It's covered in moss, dead insects and large bones. Your torch allows you to see broken arrows, rusty swords and skeletal remains, destroyed and defaced by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a ghostly area. Spiderwebs cover everything, large figures seem to be wrapped in the same web. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass countless passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive granite door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're pretty sure you're being watched.
A small dark cave in a somber swamp marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the dark cave lies a modest, shady room. It's covered in dirt, moss and broken pottery. Your torch allows you to see weapons racks and locked crates, destroyed and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a dark area. It's packed with boxes full of runes and magical equipment, as well as skeletons. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass many different passages, some are dead ends, others lead to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide wooden door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. is that a scratching sound coming from behind the door?
A tall overgrown boulder in a sinister morass marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a narrow, damp room. It's covered in dead vermin, rat droppings and cobwebs. Your torch allows you to see broken vats and flasks, destroyed and drained by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed several empty rooms and soon you enter a ragged area. Several cages hold skeletal remains of various animals. Next to the cages are odd machines. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass a few more rooms and passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge metal door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. something just grabbed your shoulder.

Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a filthy area. Spiderwebs cover everything, large figures seem to be wrapped in the same web. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass a few more passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A tall granite door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.
A modest fallen temple in a bleak mountain top marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen temple lies a massive, timeworn room. It's covered in rat droppings, puddles of water and remains. Your torch allows you to see rows of vertical tombs, long lost and ravished by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a ragged area. There's a seemingly endless hole in the center. Around it are what seem like runes. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, each seem to go on forever, leading to who knows what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge wooden door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.

Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a worn area. Small holes and carved paths cover the walls, it looks like a community or burrow for small creatures. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a clammy area. Small holes and carved paths cover the walls, it looks like a community or burrow for small creatures. What happened in this place? You proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass countless passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A tall wooden door blocks your path. Strange writing is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did somebody just knock on the door?
A short crypt in a dire grove marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the crypt lies a large, foggy room. It's covered in ash, rat droppings and ash. Your torch allows you to see what seems like some form of a sacrificial chamber, wasted and consumed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a grimy area. There's a seemingly endless hole in the center. Around it are what seem like runes. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass various passages, some look awfully familiar, others stranger everything else. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A grand granite door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A grand graveyard in a grim marsh marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the graveyard lies a modest, foggy room. It's covered in bat droppings, dead insects and crawling insects. Your torch allows you to see cases of explosives and mining equipment, wasted and dismantled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a filthy area. It's filled with hanging cages which still hold skeletal remains. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass various passages, some of them have collapsed, others seem to go on forever. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious metal door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did something just move behind this door?
A narrow murky cave in a eerie marsh marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the murky cave lies a grand, timeworn room. It's covered in dead insects, small bones and remains. Your torch allows you to see empty chests and broken statues, tattered and claimed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a foggy area. Remnants of a makeshift barricade still 'guard' the group of skeletons behind it. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass many rooms and passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge metal door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.

Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a dusty area. There's a round stone in the center, around it are a dozen skeletons in a circle. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass many rooms and passages, some of them have collapsed, others seem to go on forever. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous granite door blocks your path. Countless runes are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did somebody just knock on the door?

Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a humid area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass a few more passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A vast granite door blocks your path. Countless runes are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. Its twisted trail leads passed several empty rooms and soon you enter a dark area. Several stacks of gunpowder barrels are stacked against a wall. A skeleton holding a torch lies before it. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass many rooms and passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a shady area. There's a round stone in the center, around it are a dozen skeletons in a circle. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, each leading to who knows where, or what. A short worn statue in a sinister woodlands marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the worn statue lies a modest, putrid room. It's covered in remains, moss and dead insects. Your torch allows you to see rows of statues, forgotten and claimed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the middle. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a humid area. It's filled with tombs, but their owners are spread across the floor. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass many different passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick granite door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.

You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous wooden door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.

You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous granite door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A narrow overgrown boulder in a foggy swamp marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a narrow, weary room. It's covered in moss, broken pottery and dirt. Your torch allows you to see remnants of statues, weathered and consumed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the middle. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a ragged area. The floor is riddled with shredded blue prints and a half finished machine sits in a corner. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass a few more passages, most of which probably lead to other depths of this dungeon. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive metal door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. what was that sound?

You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're sure you saw a shadow under the cracks of the door.
A modest fallen tree in a overcast grove marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tree lies a massive, damp room. It's covered in dead vermin, cobwebs and puddles of water. Your torch allows you to see carved out openings filled with pottery, deteriorated and eaten by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a worn area. There's machinery all over the place, probably part of a workshop of sorts. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass countless passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge granite door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.

A massive waterfall in a overcast thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the waterfall lies a scanty, crumbling room. It's covered in puddles of water, bat droppings and broken stone. Your torch allows you to see broken cages and torture devices, battered and defaced by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a dank area. Spiderwebs cover everything, large figures seem to be wrapped in the same web. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass countless passages, each with their own twists, turns and destinations. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A vast metal door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.

Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a ragged area. It's filled with strange glowing crystals and countless dead vermin. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass a few more rooms and passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious wooden door blocks your path. Ash and soot is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A grand fallen tree in a gloomy marsh marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tree lies a massive, worn room. It's covered in remains, small bones and dead vermin. Your torch allows you to see warped and molten metal remnants, wasted and absorbed by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a dark area. It's filled with strange glowing crystals and countless dead vermin. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass many rooms and passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious metal door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're sure you saw a shadow under the cracks of the door.
A large waterfall in a dark mountain base marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the waterfall lies a large, ragged room. It's covered in ash, cobwebs and broken pottery. Your torch allows you to see empty shelves and broken pots, long lost and mutilated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a crumbled area. The floor is riddled with shredded blue prints and a half finished machine sits in a corner. What happened in this place? You carefully continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass a few more rooms and passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge wooden door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. is that a scratching sound coming from behind the door?
A wide fallen tree in a grim marsh marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tree lies a large, dank room. It's covered in broken stone, broken stone and cobwebs. Your torch allows you to see rows of tombs and several statues, busted and ravaged by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a ghastly area. An altar in the center is covered in runes, some of which are glowing. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass countless passages, most of which have collapsed or were dead ends to begin with. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious granite door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A narrow fallen tower in a foggy snowland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tower lies a scanty, putrid room. It's covered in bat droppings, dirt and dead insects. Your torch allows you to see what seems like some form of a sacrificial chamber, worn and absorbed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a ghostly area. It's filled with tombs, but their owners are spread across the floor. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass countless passages, they all look so similar, this whole place is a maze. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A grand granite door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.

Its twisted trail leads passed several empty rooms and soon you enter a crumbled area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass a few more passages, each leading to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. Your torch allows you to see prison cells, weathered and consumed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a timeworn area. It's littered with skeletons, but no weaponry in sight. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, most of which have collapsed or were dead ends to begin with. A grand broken temple in a overcast thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken temple lies a scanty, putrid room. It's covered in small bones, broken stone and puddles of water. Your torch allows you to see remnants of sacks, crates and caskets, worn down and mutilated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed collapsed rooms and pillaged treasuries and soon you enter a filthy area. There's a seemingly endless hole in the center. Around it are what seem like runes. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass countless passages, some look awfully familiar, others stranger everything else. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A vast metal door blocks your path. Ash and soot is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did something just move behind this door?

Your torch allows you to see broken vats and flasks, weathered and absorbed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the middle. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a ghostly area. Remnants of a makeshift barricade still 'guard' the group of skeletons behind it. What happened in this place? You carefully continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, some are dead ends, others lead to who knows where, or what. A narrow fallen tower in a shadowy swamp marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tower lies a narrow, weary room. It's covered in rat droppings, cobwebs and roots. Your torch allows you to see an altar, tattered and claimed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a weary area. Several stacks of gunpowder barrels are stacked against a wall. A skeleton holding a torch lies before it. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass various passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick granite door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.

Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a dusty area. It's filled with hanging cages which still hold skeletal remains. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass many different passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous granite door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're pretty sure you're being watched.
A small pair of worn statues in a murky mountain top marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the pair of worn statues lies a scanty, timeworn room. It's covered in broken pottery, large bones and crawling insects. Your torch allows you to see broken cages and torture devices, wasted and spoiled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a foggy area. Several stacks of gunpowder barrels are stacked against a wall. A skeleton holding a torch lies before it. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass countless passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive granite door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did somebody just knock on the door?
A short pair of worn statues in a gloomy morass marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the pair of worn statues lies a grand, deteriorated room. It's covered in moss, small bones and moss. Your torch allows you to see warped and molten metal remnants, weathered and claimed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a ragged area. There's machinery all over the place, probably part of a workshop of sorts. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass various passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A big wooden door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're sure you saw a shadow under the cracks of the door.
A grand overgrown boulder in a murky wasteland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a large, filthy room. It's covered in roots, cobwebs and dead vermin. Your torch allows you to see a pillaged treasury, pillaged and wiped out by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a ragged area. There's a pile of skeletons in the center, all burned and black. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass a few more passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.
A tall fallen temple in a eerie bog marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen temple lies a grand, dusty room. It's covered in large bones, cobwebs and remains. Your torch allows you to see remnants of a small camp, long lost and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed collapsed rooms and pillaged treasuries and soon you enter a putrid area. Spiderwebs cover everything, large figures seem to be wrapped in the same web. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass many different passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive granite door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. is that a scratching sound coming from behind the door?
A small boulder in a dire bog marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the boulder lies a grand, putrid room. It's covered in rubble, small bones and broken pottery. Your torch allows you to see remnants of statues, worn down and defaced by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a foggy area. There's a round stone in the center, around it are a dozen skeletons in a circle. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass countless passages, each seem to go on forever, leading to who knows what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide metal door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A grand graveyard in a foggy grove marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the graveyard lies a modest, shady room. It's covered in large bones, dead vermin and small bones. Your torch allows you to see remnants of statues, decayed and spoiled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed collapsed rooms and pillaged treasuries and soon you enter a foggy area. There's a huge skeleton in the center, along with dozens of human skeletons. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass a few more passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge granite door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you think you can hear a whisper coming from behind the door.
A wide broken statue in a gloomy bog marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken statue lies a scanty, crumbling room. It's covered in dirt, puddles of water and remains. Your torch allows you to see a broken tomb, battered and absorbed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a timeworn area. The room is filled with lifelike statues of terrified people. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass many rooms and passages, each with their own twists, turns and destinations. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An enormous wooden door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.
A tall waterfall in a misty mountain top marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the waterfall lies a large, worn room. It's covered in cobwebs, remains and large bones. Your torch allows you to see empty shelves and broken pots, wasted and taken by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed collapsed rooms and pillaged treasuries and soon you enter a dark area. It's packed with boxes full of runes and magical equipment, as well as skeletons. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass many rooms and passages, some are dead ends, others lead to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide wooden door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.

You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.
A narrow graveyard in a somber snowland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the graveyard lies a scanty, dank room. It's covered in small bones, broken pottery and dead insects. Your torch allows you to see an overgrown underground garden, pillaged and eaten by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a crumbled area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You carefully continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass many different passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A big metal door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did something just move behind this door?

A wide metal door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. what was that sound?

A massive boulder in a misty mountain top marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the boulder lies a large, grimy room. It's covered in ash, roots and roots. Your torch allows you to see empty shelves and broken pots, worn and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed several empty rooms and soon you enter a shady area. It's littered with skeletons, but no weaponry in sight. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, most of which have collapsed or were dead ends to begin with. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide wooden door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.

A wide murky cave in a eerie cliff side marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the murky cave lies a small, foggy room. It's covered in ash, broken pottery and roots. Your torch allows you to see a broken tomb, battered and eaten by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a humid area. There's machinery all over the place, probably part of a workshop of sorts. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, they all look so similar, this whole place is a maze. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A large metal door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.

Your torch allows you to see empty chests and broken statues, weathered and dismantled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a weary area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass many rooms and passages, some are dead ends, others lead to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A big granite door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. what was that sound?
A narrow murky cave in a shady wasteland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the murky cave lies a grand, dark room. It's covered in small bones, dirt and crawling insects. Your torch allows you to see what seems like some form of a sacrificial chamber, demolished and ravaged by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a ghostly area. It's littered with skeletons, but no weaponry in sight. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass a few more passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A vast wooden door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.

A massive boulder in a somber mountain range marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the boulder lies a large, timeworn room. It's covered in cobwebs, rubble and cobwebs. Your torch allows you to see rows of vertical tombs, pillaged and drained by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a filthy area. Countless traps, swinging axes and other devices move all around. They're either still active, or just activated. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're pretty sure you're being watched.

Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a crumbled area. Several cages hold skeletal remains of various animals. Next to the cages are odd machines. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.

A minor fallen tree in a somber morass marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tree lies a massive, weary room. It's covered in roots, moss and ash. Your torch allows you to see ruins of what seems to be a crude throne room, demolished and defaced by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a humid area. Remnants of a makeshift barricade still 'guard' the group of skeletons behind it. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An enormous wooden door blocks your path. Strange writing is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.

It's covered in puddles of water, cobwebs and broken stone. Your torch allows you to see an altar, pillaged and eaten by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a damp area. It's packed with boxes full of runes and magical equipment, as well as skeletons. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass various passages, they all look so similar, this whole place is a maze. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive granite door blocks your path. Strange writing is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you think you can hear a whisper coming from behind the door.

What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, some look awfully familiar, others stranger everything else. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A tall metal door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.
A large broken temple in a eerie bog marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken temple lies a modest, dank room. It's covered in broken stone, moss and roots. Your torch allows you to see warped and molten metal remnants, forgotten and claimed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a timeworn area. It's filled with hanging cages which still hold skeletal remains. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass many rooms and passages, each seem to go on forever, leading to who knows what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An immense wooden door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. something just grabbed your shoulder.

You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass various passages, some of them have collapsed, others seem to go on forever. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge wooden door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.

Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a ghastly area. It's packed with boxes full of runes and magical equipment, as well as skeletons. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass countless passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A large metal door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.
A small pair of granite doors in a shadowy swamp marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the pair of granite doors lies a small, ragged room. It's covered in moss, moss and dirt. Your torch allows you to see broken vats and flasks, tattered and claimed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a shady area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, some of them have collapsed, others seem to go on forever. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.
A large worn statue in a shadowy mountain top marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the worn statue lies a grand, shady room. It's covered in bat droppings, roots and dead vermin. Your torch allows you to see remnants of what once must've been a mess hall of sorts, forgotten and claimed by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a damp area. There are several braziers scattered around, somehow they're still burning, or burning again. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass a few more passages, some are dead ends, others lead to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious metal door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did something just move behind this door?
A wide granite door in a shady cliff side marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the granite door lies a narrow, timeworn room. It's covered in remains, large bones and cobwebs. Your torch allows you to see prison cells, long lost and mutilated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a foggy area. Countless traps, swinging axes and other devices move all around. They're either still active, or just activated. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass countless passages, each leading to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous wooden door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did something just move behind this door?
A massive pair of worn statues in a dark bog marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the pair of worn statues lies a large, humid room. It's covered in puddles of water, broken pottery and dead vermin. Your torch allows you to see prison cells, destroyed and desolated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a damp area. There's a pile of skeletons in the center, all burned and black. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass many different passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive granite door blocks your path. Ash and soot is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you think you can hear a whisper coming from behind the door.
A wide murky cave in a somber marsh marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the murky cave lies a small, shady room. It's covered in rat droppings, bat droppings and small bones. Your torch allows you to see warped and molten metal remnants, wasted and maimed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a humid area. Small holes and carved paths cover the walls, it looks like a community or burrow for small creatures. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass many different passages, each leading to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick granite door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.

Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a grimy area. It's littered with skeletons, but no weaponry in sight. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass various passages, some look awfully familiar, others stranger everything else. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A tall metal door blocks your path. Strange writing is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.

Your torch allows you to see drawings and symbols on the walls, tattered and desolated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a damp area. It's filled with tombs, some of which no longer hold their owner. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass many rooms and passages, each with their own twists, turns and destinations. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A large granite door blocks your path. Countless runes are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. is that a scratching sound coming from behind the door?

You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're sure you saw a shadow under the cracks of the door.

Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a dank area. There's a seemingly endless hole in the center. Around it are what seem like runes. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass a few more passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide metal door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.
A wide worn statue in a dire bog marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the worn statue lies a grand, weary room. It's covered in rat droppings, rubble and dirt. Your torch allows you to see triggered traps and skeletal remains, decayed and eaten by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the middle. Its twisted trail leads passed several empty rooms and soon you enter a weary area. It's filled with tombs, but their owners are spread across the floor. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass many rooms and passages, each with their own twists, turns and destinations. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An immense wooden door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.
A minor fallen tower in a bleak snowland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tower lies a small, grimy room. It's covered in rubble, remains and dead vermin. Your torch allows you to see a pillaged treasury, long lost and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a putrid area. There's a round stone in the center, around it are a dozen skeletons in a circle. What happened in this place? You carefully continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass a few more rooms and passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A big metal door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. was that a growl coming from behind the door?
A narrow broken statue in a gloomy marsh marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken statue lies a modest, clammy room. It's covered in cobwebs, bat droppings and dead insects. Your torch allows you to see empty shelves and broken pots, battered and drained by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a ragged area. The floor is riddled with shredded blue prints and a half finished machine sits in a corner. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass many rooms and passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious metal door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.
A modest waterfall in a shadowy boulder field marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the waterfall lies a massive, filthy room. It's covered in roots, small bones and ash. Your torch allows you to see an altar, busted and ravaged by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a clammy area. The room is filled with lifelike statues of terrified people. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass many rooms and passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did something just move behind this door?
A wide waterfall in a sinister morass marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the waterfall lies a massive, broken room. It's covered in broken stone, small bones and moss. Your torch allows you to see drawings and symbols on the walls, decayed and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a worn area. The floor is riddled with shredded blue prints and a half finished machine sits in a corner. What happened in this place? You carefully continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass countless passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious granite door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.
A modest fallen tree in a gloomy boulder field marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tree lies a modest, dank room. It's covered in crawling insects, cobwebs and small bones. Your torch allows you to see locked chests, vats, crates and pieces of broken wood, busted and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a clammy area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass many rooms and passages, most of which probably lead to other depths of this dungeon. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A large wooden door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A grand fallen tree in a eerie mountain range marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tree lies a large, broken room. It's covered in broken pottery, rubble and rubble. Your torch allows you to see remnants of sacks, crates and caskets, worn and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a ghastly area. Countless traps, swinging axes and other devices move all around. They're either still active, or just activated. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass many different passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide metal door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A small overgrown boulder in a overcast cliff side marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a large, clammy room. It's covered in large bones, puddles of water and bat droppings. Your torch allows you to see carved out openings filled with pottery, busted and ravished by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a ghostly area. It's littered with skeletons, but no weaponry in sight. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass countless passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A tall granite door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. what was that sound?

Your torch allows you to see the remnants of a pillaged burial chamber, aged and maimed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a putrid area. Small holes and carved paths cover the walls, it looks like a community or burrow for small creatures. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass a few more rooms and passages, some are dead ends, others lead to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A big metal door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.

It's covered in crawling insects, small bones and cobwebs. Your torch allows you to see remnants of what was once a decorated room with a now unknown purpose, decayed and consumed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the middle. Its twisted trail leads passed collapsed rooms and pillaged treasuries and soon you enter a weary area. It's filled with tombs, but their owners are spread across the floor. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass many rooms and passages, some are dead ends, others seem to have no end at all. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous wooden door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. was that a growl coming from behind the door?

Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a humid area. There's a demolished door with a sign that says "don't open". What happened in this place? You proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secret passages. You pass many different passages, most of which probably lead to other depths of this dungeon. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious wooden door blocks your path. Ash and soot is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A grand granite door in a somber thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the granite door lies a scanty, grimy room. It's covered in ash, cobwebs and broken pottery. Your torch allows you to see weapons racks and locked crates, decayed and consumed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a dank area. Piles and piles of gold lie in the center, several skeletons lie next to it. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass a few more rooms and passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick metal door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did somebody just knock on the door?
A grand fallen temple in a grim mountain base marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen temple lies a modest, worn room. It's covered in small bones, large bones and moss. Your torch allows you to see prison cells, worn and mutilated by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the middle. Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a ghostly area. There's a round stone in the center, around it are a dozen skeletons in a circle. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass many rooms and passages, most lead to nowhere or back to this same path. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous granite door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A grand overgrown boulder in a shadowy mountain top marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a narrow, timeworn room. It's covered in roots, remains and ash. Your torch allows you to see locked chests, vats, crates and pieces of broken wood, worn down and spoiled by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed broken and pillaged tombs and soon you enter a putrid area. There are several braziers scattered around, somehow they're still burning, or burning again. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass many rooms and passages, most of which have collapsed or were dead ends to begin with. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An immense wooden door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A modest broken statue in a overcast thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken statue lies a narrow, filthy room. It's covered in ash, broken stone and ash. Your torch allows you to see remnants of sacks, crates and caskets, weathered and spoiled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a damp area. Spiderwebs cover everything, large figures seem to be wrapped in the same web. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass various passages, some look awfully familiar, others stranger everything else. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An enormous wooden door blocks your path. Strange writing is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A short fallen tower in a shady woodlands marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tower lies a large, timeworn room. It's covered in crawling insects, broken pottery and moss. Your torch allows you to see a pillaged treasury, frayed and desolated by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a ghastly area. Several stacks of gunpowder barrels are stacked against a wall. A skeleton holding a torch lies before it. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass many rooms and passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A vast granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A modest broken statue in a dark morass marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken statue lies a large, weary room. It's covered in dead insects, dead insects and cobwebs. Your torch allows you to see the remnants of a pillaged burial chamber, long lost and defaced by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a filthy area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, each seem to go on forever, leading to who knows what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive granite door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.

Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a putrid area. Countless traps, swinging axes and other devices move all around. They're either still active, or just activated. What happened in this place? You tread onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, they all look so similar, this whole place is a maze. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a dark area. Piles and piles of gold lie in the center, several skeletons lie next to it. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, each seem to go on forever, leading to who knows what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious granite door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.
A minor overgrown boulder in a eerie wasteland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a narrow, dank room. It's covered in rubble, cobwebs and ash. Your torch allows you to see rows of tombs and several statues, worn and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a ghastly area. Countless traps, swinging axes and other devices move all around. They're either still active, or just activated. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass a few more rooms and passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide wooden door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did something just move behind this door?
A tall graveyard in a somber mountain base marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the graveyard lies a scanty, grimy room. It's covered in broken stone, dead insects and large bones. Your torch allows you to see rows of statues, battered and absorbed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a foggy area. There's a seemingly endless hole in the center. Around it are what seem like runes. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass a few more rooms and passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. something just grabbed your shoulder.
A small overgrown boulder in a foggy grove marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a scanty, deteriorated room. It's covered in broken pottery, dirt and roots. Your torch allows you to see broken vats and flasks, long lost and eaten by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a dark area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, they all look so similar, this whole place is a maze. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A tall granite door blocks your path. Countless odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're sure you saw a shadow under the cracks of the door.
A minor fallen tree in a dark mountain range marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen tree lies a scanty, clammy room. It's covered in cobwebs, rubble and rubble. Your torch allows you to see what seems like some form of a sacrificial chamber, worn down and eaten by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a shady area. It's packed with boxes full of runes and magical equipment, as well as skeletons. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass countless passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An immense wooden door blocks your path. Countless runes are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. is that a scratching sound coming from behind the door?
A modest overgrown boulder in a gloomy wasteland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the overgrown boulder lies a modest, damp room. It's covered in broken pottery, roots and large bones. Your torch allows you to see ruins of what seems to be a crude throne room, wasted and drained by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads passed several empty rooms and soon you enter a dusty area. There's a seemingly endless hole in the center. Around it are what seem like runes. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass many different passages, each with their own twists, turns and destinations. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An ominous wooden door blocks your path. Strange writing is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. did the door just change its appearance?
A minor broken temple in a dark boulder field marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken temple lies a grand, timeworn room. It's covered in dead insects, small bones and ash. Your torch allows you to see remnants of what once must've been a mess hall of sorts, tattered and consumed by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a ghostly area. There's machinery all over the place, probably part of a workshop of sorts. What happened in this place? You carefully continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass many different passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A tall metal door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. what was that sound?
A narrow graveyard in a murky thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the graveyard lies a scanty, grimy room. It's covered in crawling insects, crawling insects and rat droppings. Your torch allows you to see drawings and symbols on the walls, worn down and butchered by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed countless other pathways and soon you enter a shady area. It's filled with hanging cages which still hold skeletal remains. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass many rooms and passages, most of which probably lead to other depths of this dungeon. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious wooden door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.

Your torch allows you to see prison cells, tattered and butchered by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the left is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a weary area. It's packed with boxes full of runes and magical equipment, as well as skeletons. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass many different passages, some of them have collapsed, others seem to go on forever. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge metal door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.

It's covered in rat droppings, puddles of water and broken stone. Your torch allows you to see remnants of what was once a decorated room with a now unknown purpose, worn and claimed by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a shady area. An enormous beastly skeleton is chained to the walls. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass a few more passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A wide granite door blocks your path. Strange writing is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're sure you saw a shadow under the cracks of the door.
