Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a ghastly area. Countless traps, swinging axes and other devices move all around. They're either still active, or just activated. What happened in this place? You cautiously proceed onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass a few more rooms and passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick wooden door blocks your path. Dire warning messages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. was that a growl coming from behind the door?
A wide broken statue in a murky snowland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the broken statue lies a narrow, crumbling room. It's covered in broken pottery, puddles of water and rat droppings. Your torch allows you to see broken mining equipment, frayed and consumed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed several empty rooms and soon you enter a putrid area. Small holes and carved paths cover the walls, it looks like a community or burrow for small creatures. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, most of which have collapsed or were dead ends to begin with. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An enormous wooden door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. light's coming through the gap below the door.
A narrow boulder in a shady forest marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the boulder lies a small, humid room. It's covered in rubble, rubble and large bones. Your torch allows you to see broken vats and flasks, destroyed and drained by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a clammy area. The floor is riddled with shredded blue prints and a half finished machine sits in a corner. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass countless passages, each seem to go on forever, leading to who knows what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge wooden door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. was that a growl coming from behind the door?
A wide fallen temple in a grim swamp marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen temple lies a massive, timeworn room. It's covered in broken stone, roots and moss. Your torch allows you to see remnants of what once must've been a mess hall of sorts, pillaged and dismantled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a worn area. It's filled with strange glowing crystals and countless dead vermin. What happened in this place? You continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass countless passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A huge wooden door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. something just grabbed your shoulder.
A narrow boulder in a eerie snowland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the boulder lies a scanty, deteriorated room. It's covered in moss, roots and ash. Your torch allows you to see empty shelves and broken pots, pillaged and mutilated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, but the right is a dead end. Its twisted trail leads passed long lost rooms and tombs and soon you enter a weary area. Piles and piles of gold lie in the center, several skeletons lie next to it. What happened in this place? You advance carefully onwards, deeper into the dungeon's secrets. You pass a few more rooms and passages, some have collapsed, others are dead ends or too dangerous to try. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A massive wooden door blocks your path. Messages in strange languages are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're sure you saw a shadow under the cracks of the door.
A large crypt in a somber swamp marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the crypt lies a modest, crumbling room. It's covered in roots, bat droppings and broken stone. Your torch allows you to see rows of tombs and several statues, frayed and maimed by time itself. Further ahead are three paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed pillaged rooms and soon you enter a ghastly area. Spiderwebs cover everything, large figures seem to be wrapped in the same web. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass a few more rooms and passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A grand granite door blocks your path. Ominous symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. something just grabbed your shoulder.
A minor dark cave in a dire cliff side marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the dark cave lies a narrow, humid room. It's covered in roots, large bones and ash. Your torch allows you to see what seems like some form of a sacrificial chamber, demolished and wrecked by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the right. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a putrid area. Several cages hold skeletal remains of various animals. Next to the cages are odd machines. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's mysteries. You pass countless passages, most of which look just like the other. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A large metal door blocks your path. Various odd symbols are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you're pretty sure you're being watched.
A grand fallen temple in a somber woods marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen temple lies a small, worn room. It's covered in rubble, rubble and cobwebs. Your torch allows you to see a broken tomb, long lost and desolated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads downwards and soon you enter a timeworn area. There are several braziers scattered around, somehow they're still burning, or burning again. What happened in this place? You press onwards, deeper into the dungeon's darkness. You pass a few more rooms and passages, each seem to go on forever, leading to who knows what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A vast wooden door blocks your path. Countless runes are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
A grand crypt in a gloomy thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the crypt lies a grand, clammy room. It's covered in rubble, rubble and moss. Your torch allows you to see broken vats and flasks, tattered and claimed by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed lost treasuries, unknown rooms and armories and soon you enter a dank area. It's filled with strange glowing crystals and countless dead vermin. What happened in this place? You carefully continue onwards, deeper into the dungeon's shadows. You pass many different passages, they all look so similar, this whole place is a maze. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A large metal door blocks your path. Intricate carvings are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a faint laugh coming from behind the door.
A large fallen temple in a shadowy snowland marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the fallen temple lies a massive, crumbling room. It's covered in puddles of water, bat droppings and dead vermin. Your torch allows you to see what seems like some form of a sacrificial chamber, pillaged and dismantled by time itself. Further ahead is a single path. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a putrid area. Several stacks of gunpowder barrels are stacked against a wall. A skeleton holding a torch lies before it. What happened in this place? You slowly march onwards, deeper into the dungeon's expanse. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, it's one big labyrinth of twists and turns. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A mysterious metal door blocks your path. Large claw marks are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear a loud bang in the distance from which you came.
A short granite door in a misty thicket marks the entrance to this dungeon. Beyond the granite door lies a modest, dank room. It's covered in rubble, ash and dead vermin. Your torch allows you to see empty chests and broken statues, busted and dismantled by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads onwards and soon you enter a filthy area. It's littered with skeletons, but no weaponry in sight. What happened in this place? You move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass dozens of similar rooms and passages, most of which are far too ominous looking to try out. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. An enormous granite door blocks your path. Dried blood splatters are all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. you hear the faint sound of footsteps behind you.

Your torch allows you to see an altar, worn and desolated by time itself. Further ahead are two paths, you take the left. Its twisted trail leads passed countless rooms and soon you enter a damp area. It's filled with strange glowing crystals and countless dead vermin. What happened in this place? You slowly move onwards, deeper into the dungeon's depths. You pass various different rooms and countless passages, some are dead ends, others lead to who knows where, or what. You eventually make it to what is likely the final room. A thick metal door blocks your path. Ash and soot is all over it, somehow untouched by time and the elements. You step closer to inspect it and.. wait.. suddenly the door slowly opens on its own.
